						include_locked = yes

					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes

							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {

								}

				}

			TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_eaeu_reform }

				has_completed_focus = generic_eaeu_reform
				has_completed_focus = major_eaeu_reform
			}}
		}

		}
